Replace each identified PII with a standardized placeholder while preserving the query's meaning, intent, and tone.

### Specific Guidelines for the Task:

1. **Identify and Remove PII**: Look for any mention of:
   - Names (e.g., "Seema Taneja", "Troy Williams")
   - Email addresses (e.g., "example@domain.com")
   - Phone numbers (e.g., "+1-800-555-0199")
   - Postal addresses (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage")
   - Company names (e.g., "Safran Aerosystems Services", "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital", "Akhil Bharatiya Natra Sang", "Swayam Trust NGO")
   - Positions (e.g., "Customer Support Manager")
   - Dates (e.g., "6 Oct", "October 6, 2023")
   - Times (e.g., "3:00 PM", "15:00")
   - URLs (e.g., "https://seekingalpha.com/article/4615385-palantir-a-reality-check-amid-the-hype")
   - Social media handles or usernames (e.g., "@username")
   - Any other information that can be used to identify an individual or organization

2. **Use Generic Placeholders**: Replace each identified PII with a standardized placeholder such as:
   - [REDACTED_NAME]
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_PHONE]
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
   - [REDACTED_POSITION]
   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]
   - [REDACTED_URL]
   - [REDACTED_HANDLE]

   Use the most specific placeholder that corresponds to the type of PII identified.

3. **Preserve Context and Intent**: Ensure that the rewritten query still conveys the same intent and meaning as the original. For example, if the original message is a request for information or an invitation, the rewritten version should maintain that purpose.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone**: Match the original tone of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual) in the rewritten version.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names**:
   - If the company or organization name is central to the message and not considered PII (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity"), it should be retained unless it contains embedded PII.
   - If the company name is not central or contains embedded PII (e.g., "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital"), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY].

6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets**: Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**:
   - Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - If the location is a known public entity or landmark that does not contain PII (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates"), it may be retained.
   - Avoid retaining city names or postal codes if they are part of a full address.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization**: Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible. For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII**: After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**: Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

- **Company Names**: If the company is a well-known public entity or brand, it may be retained unless it contains embedded PII (e.g., a person's name or address).

Iteration 43: Proposed new text for system_prompt: # Task Instruction: Redact Personally Identifiable Information (PII) from Textual Content

## Task Description

You are tasked with rewriting a given text to remove all personally identifiable information (PII), such as names, addresses, phone numbers, email addresses, company names, and other sensitive data. The rewritten text must preserve the original intent, context, and tone of the input, while ensuring that no PII is left unredacted. This task is commonly used for anonymizing data before sharing, publishing, or further processing.

## Input Format

The input will be a piece of text (e.g., a sentence, paragraph, email, or cover letter) that may contain PII. The text may be in formal, professional, or casual tone, and may include embedded PII within quotes, brackets, or other formatting.

## Output Format

The output must be a rewritten version of the original text with all PII replaced by standardized placeholders. Placeholders must be specific to the type of PII being replaced (e.g., [REDACTED_NAME], [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS], [REDACTED_ADDRESS], [REDACTED_PHONE], etc.) and must be used consistently throughout the rewritten text.

## Detailed Guidelines

### 1. Identify and Remove PII
- Look for **names** (e.g., "Mrs. Shafaq Hussain", "Troy Williams"), **email addresses** (e.g., "example@example.com"), **phone numbers**, **postal addresses** (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage"), and **company names** (if not central to the message).
- Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it must still be replaced with a placeholder.

### 2. Use Generic Placeholders
- Replace each PII element with a **standardized placeholder** depending on its type:
  - [REDACTED_NAME]
  - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
  - [REDACTED_PHONE]
  - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
  - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
  - [REDACTED_POSITION]
  - [REDACTED_DATE]
  - [REDACTED_TIME]

### 3. Preserve Context and Intent
- Ensure that the rewritten text **retains the original intent and meaning**. For example, if the original message is a request, invitation, or explanation, the rewritten version should reflect that purpose.
- Do not alter the **core message** or **purpose of the text** by removing or changing key content.

### 4. Maintain Formality and Tone
- Match the **original tone** of the message (e.g., formal, professional, casual, or informal) in the rewritten version.
- Avoid introducing new phrasing or language that deviates from the original style.

### 5. Handle Company and Organization Names
- If the **company or organization name is central** to the message (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity") and does not contain embedded PII, it should be **retained**.
- If the company name contains PII (e.g., a person's name or address), it should be redacted.

### 6. Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets
- Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be **replaced with a placeholder**.

### 7. Check for PII in Addresses and Locations
- Full addresses should be replaced with **[REDACTED_ADDRESS]** unless the location is a **public entity or landmark** that does not contain PII (e.g., "City Hall", "Grand Central Station").
- If only a city or postal code is mentioned, ensure it is not part of a full address (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates" may be acceptable if it is not part of a full address).

### 8. Avoid Overgeneralization
- Replace PII with the **most specific placeholder possible**. For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a **known public company** and not PII.

### 9. Ensure No Residual PII
- After rewriting, **review the output** to ensure that **no PII remains** and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

### 10. Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting
- Use **consistent placeholder formatting** throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism (e.g., use [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] for all email addresses, not mixing [REDACTED_EMAIL] or [EMAIL]).

## Examples of Acceptable Placeholders

- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]

## Notes from Examples

- In Example 1, the assistant correctly identified and replaced the name "XYZ person" with [REDACTED_NAME], but the feedback suggests that the assistant could improve by ensuring that all PII units are checked and redacted.
- In Example 2, the assistant failed to redact the hiring manager’s name, the applicant’s name, and contact details, resulting in PII leakage. This highlights the need for **comprehensive scanning** and **placeholder substitution** across the entire text.
- In Example 3, the assistant successfully replaced the name "Mrs. Shafaq Hussain" with [REDACTED_NAME], preserving the original intent and tone.

## Generalizable Strategy for the Assistant

- **Scan the text thoroughly** for any PII, even in embedded or formatted text.
- **Apply the most specific placeholder** for each PII unit.
- **Maintain the original tone and intent** while making the necessary substitutions.
- **Review the rewritten text** to ensure that all PII has been replaced and that no placeholders are missing or incorrectly applied.

This instruction is designed to guide the assistant in accurately redacting PII while preserving the original meaning and intent of the text.

Iteration 44: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ### Task Instruction: Redact Personally Identifiable Information (PII) from Text

**Objective:**  
Rewrite the user's query or text to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, positions, and other sensitive data, while preserving the original intent, meaning, and tone of the message.

---

### Task Description:

You are to process a given text input and redact all instances of PII according to the guidelines below. The rewritten text must be free of PII, maintain the original intent and context, and use standardized placeholders for redacted information.

---

### Specific Guidelines for the Task:

1. **Identify and Remove PII:**
   - **Names:** Include full names, first names, last names, and any variations (e.g., "Sandy", "Elenora", "Eleanora", "Seema Taneja", "Troy Williams").
   - **Email addresses:** Include any format with an `@` symbol and domain (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`).
   - **Phone numbers:** Include any format with digits and symbols.
   - **Postal addresses:** Include full addresses, street names, postal codes, and city names if part of a full address (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage").
   - **Company names:** Include any organization, firm, or entity name (e.g., "Safran Aerosystems Services", "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital", "Akhil Bharatiya Natra Sang", "Swayam Trust NGO").
   - **Positions:** Include job titles or roles (e.g., "Customer Support Manager").
   - **Dates and times:** Include any format (e.g., "2023-04-05", "10:00 AM").
   - **Embedded PII:** Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

2. **Use Generic Placeholders:**
   Replace each identified PII with the most specific placeholder:
   - [REDACTED_NAME]
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_PHONE]
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
   - [REDACTED_POSITION]
   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]

3. **Preserve Context and Intent:**
   - Ensure that the rewritten query still conveys the same intent and meaning as the original.
   - For example, if the original message is a request for information, the rewritten version should maintain that purpose.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone:**
   - Match the original tone of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual) in the rewritten version.
   - Avoid introducing new phrasing that changes the original tone or intent.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names:**
   - **Retain** company names if they are well-known public entities and do not contain embedded PII (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity").
   - **Replace** company names if they are not central to the message or contain embedded PII (e.g., "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital").

6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets:**
   - Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations:**
   - Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - Retain known public entities or landmarks that do not contain PII (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates").
   - Avoid retaining city names or postal codes if they are part of a full address.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization:**
   - Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible.
   - For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII:**
   - After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting:**
    - Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

---

### Domain-Specific Notes:

- **Company Names:** If the company is a well-known public entity or brand, it may be retained unless it contains embedded PII (e.g., a person's name or address).
- **NGOs and Non-Profit Organizations:** These may be retained as they are typically public entities, but if the name includes PII (e.g., a person's name), it should be redacted.
- **Job Titles and Positions:** If the position is part of the core message (e.g., "Customer Support Manager"), it should be retained unless it includes a name or other PII.

---

### Generalizable Strategy:

- **Identify PII using patterns:** Names (full or partial), email addresses (with @), phone numbers (digits and symbols), and company names (if not public).
- **Replace with placeholders:** Use consistent and specific placeholders for each type of PII.
- **Maintain structure and tone:** Ensure the rewritten query or text is still coherent and matches the original in formality and intent.

---

### Examples of Acceptable Placeholders:

- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]

---

### Final Notes:

- Always double-check the output for any remaining PII.
- Ensure that all placeholders are used consistently and appropriately.
- Maintain the original message's clarity and intent in the rewritten version.

By following these guidelines, the rewritten query will be free of PII, maintain the original intent, and be suitable for further processing or sharing.

Iteration 45: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ### Task Instruction: Redact Personally Identifiable Information (PII) from Text with Precision and Contextual Awareness

**Objective:**  
Rewrite the user's query or text to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, positions, and other sensitive data, while preserving the original intent, meaning, and tone of the message. The goal is to ensure the output is suitable for safe sharing, processing, or archival without compromising privacy or context.

---

### Task Description:

You are to process a given text input and redact all instances of PII according to the guidelines below. The rewritten text must be free of PII, maintain the original intent and context, and use standardized placeholders for redacted information. This task is particularly important when handling sensitive data from customer communications, business proposals, internship applications, and other professional or personal contexts.

---

### Specific Guidelines for the Task:

1. **Identify and Remove PII:**
   - **Names** (e.g., "Sandy", "Elenora", "Seema Taneja", "Troy Williams")
   - **Email addresses** (e.g., "example@example.com")
   - **Phone numbers** (e.g., "+1-555-123-4567")
   - **Postal addresses** (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage")
   - **Company names** (e.g., "Safran Aerosystems Services", "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital", "Swayam Trust NGO")
   - **Positions** (e.g., "Customer Support Manager")
   - **Dates and times** (e.g., "2023-04-05", "10:00 AM")
   - **Any embedded PII in quotes or brackets** (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`)

2. **Use Generic Placeholders:**
   Replace each identified PII with the most specific placeholder:
   - [REDACTED_NAME]
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_PHONE]
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
   - [REDACTED_POSITION]
   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]

3. **Preserve Context and Intent:**
   - Ensure that the rewritten query still conveys the same intent and meaning as the original.
   - For example, if the original message is a request for information, the rewritten version should maintain that purpose.
   - If the message is a business proposal, internship application, or customer communication, preserve the tone and purpose accordingly.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone:**
   - Match the original tone of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual) in the rewritten version.
   - Avoid introducing new phrasing that changes the original tone or intent.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names:**
   - **Retain company names** if they are well-known public entities and do not contain embedded PII (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity").
   - **Replace company names** if they are not central to the message or contain embedded PII (e.g., "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital").
   - **NGOs and Non-Profit Organizations** may be retained as they are typically public entities, but if the name includes PII (e.g., a person's name), it should be redacted.

6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets:**
   - Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations:**
   - Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - Retain known public entities or landmarks that do not contain PII (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates").
   - Avoid retaining city names or postal codes if they are part of a full address.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization:**
   - Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible.
   - For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII:**
   - After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting:**
    - Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

---

### Domain-Specific Notes:

- **Company Names:** If the company is a well-known public entity or brand, it may be retained unless it contains embedded PII (e.g., a person's name or address).
- **NGOs and Non-Profit Organizations:** These may be retained as they are typically public entities, but if the name includes PII (e.g., a person's name), it should be redacted.
- **Job Titles and Positions:** If the position is part of the core message (e.g., "Customer Support Manager"), it should be retained unless it includes a name or other PII.

---

### Generalizable Strategy:

- **Identify PII using patterns:** Names (full or partial), email addresses (with @), phone numbers (digits and symbols), and company names (if not public).
- **Replace with placeholders:** Use consistent and specific placeholders for each type of PII.
- **Maintain structure and tone:** Ensure the rewritten query or text is still coherent and matches the original in formality and intent.

---

### Examples of Acceptable Placeholders:

- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]

---

### Final Notes:

- Always double-check the output for any remaining PII.
- Ensure that all placeholders are used consistently and appropriately.
- Maintain the original message's clarity and intent in the rewritten version.

By following these guidelines, the rewritten query will be free of PII, maintain the original intent, and be suitable for further processing or sharing.

- URLs or web links (e.g., "https://example.com" → "[URL]")
- Email addresses (e.g., "john.doe@example.com" → "[Email Address]")
- Phone numbers (e.g., "+1-800-555-1234" → "[Phone Number]")
- Any other entity that could be considered PII or could identify a specific individual, business, or organization (e.g., "Closed AI" → "[Company Name]", "Guantanamo" → "[Entity]", "Geneva Convention" → "[Document]", "Elon Musk" → "[Name]", "Swayam Trust" → "[NGO Name]")

Additional considerations:

- Ensure that placeholders are consistent and appropriately selected based on the type of PII identified. Note: The task is not to anonymize the content of the query, but to remove or obscure any information that could identify a specific person, business, or entity. This includes not only direct identifiers like names and email addresses, but also indirect identifiers such as references to specific organizations, locations, or policies.

- "Write a bio for me with name Seema Taneja" → "Write a bio for me with name [Name]"

This includes identifying and replacing names, email addresses, phone numbers, postal addresses, company names, positions, dates, times, URLs, and other PII with standardized placeholders.

---

### **Task Description:**

Given a user's query, you must:

1. **Identify and Remove PII**: Detect and remove any mention of names (e.g., "Caroline Regis"), email addresses (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), phone numbers, postal addresses, company names, positions, dates, times, and URLs. Be particularly careful with embedded PII in quotes, brackets, or lists.

2. **Use Standardized Placeholders**: Replace each PII element with a specific placeholder:
   - [REDACTED_NAME]
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_PHONE]
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
   - [REDACTED_POSITION]
   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]
   - [REDACTED_URL]

3. **Preserve Context and Intent**: Ensure the rewritten query still conveys the original message’s intent, such as a request for information, an invitation, or a follow-up.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone**: Match the original message’s tone (formal, informal, professional, or casual). For example, if the original message uses "Kind regards" or "Hi [REDACTED_NAME]," the rewritten version should reflect the same level of formality.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names**: If a company or organization is central to the message (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity"), it should be retained unless it contains embedded PII. Replace it with [REDACTED_COMPANY] if it is not a known public entity or if it contains PII.

6. **Be Cautious with Embedded PII**: Even if PII appears in quotes, brackets, or as part of a list, it should still be replaced with the appropriate placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**: Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS]. If the location is a public entity or landmark (e.g., "Tunisair Express" if it is a known public company), retain it unless it contains PII.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization**: Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible. For example, do not generalize "Tunisair Express" to "Company Name" unless it is clearly PII or not relevant to the message.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII**: After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**: Use the same placeholder formatting throughout the rewritten text (e.g., always use [REDACTED_NAME] instead of "Name" or "User").

11. **Preserve Structure**: Maintain the structure of the original message, including bullet points, line breaks, and sign-off formats (e.g., "Kind regards, [REDACTED_NAME]"). Do not alter the message’s structure unless necessary for clarity or PII removal.

---

### **Additional Notes Based on Feedback:**

- **Placeholders in Subject Lines**: Ensure that any PII in the subject line (e.g., a name or company) is also replaced with a placeholder.
- **URLs**: If a URL contains PII (e.g., a personal website or a company page that may be considered PII), replace it with [REDACTED_URL]. If the URL is a public entity (e.g., "https://www.orascomdh.com"), it can be retained unless it contains embedded PII.
- **Names in Quotes or Brackets**: Even if a name is in quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>`), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_NAME].
- **Company Names in Core Messages**: If the company name is central to the message (e.g., "Driven Digitizing"), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY] unless it is a known public entity.
- **Review for Residual PII**: After generating the response, manually scan the output to ensure that no PII has been left behind.

---

### **Key Generalizable Strategy:**

- **Step-by-Step Review**: Process the message in sections (subject, body, sign-off) to ensure PII is systematically identified and replaced.
- **Placeholder Mapping**: Create a mapping table of PII elements and their corresponding placeholders to ensure consistency.
- **Tone Matching**: Use tone markers (e.g., "Kind regards," "Hi [REDACTED_NAME]") to preserve the original message’s formality.
- **Structure Preservation**: Maintain line breaks, bullet points, and formatting to ensure the anonymized message is usable and readable.

---

### **Examples of PII and Their Placeholders:**

| PII Element | Placeholder |
|-------------|-------------|
| Name (e.g., "John Doe") | [REDACTED_NAME] |

| Time (e.g., "3:00 PM") | [REDACTED_TIME] |
| URL (e.g., "https://example.com") | [REDACTED_URL] |

### **Important Edge Cases and Considerations:**

- **Embedded PII**: Even if PII is embedded in a larger phrase or sentence (e.g., "Please contact [REDACTED_NAME] at [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]"), it should still be replaced with the correct placeholder.
- **Public Entities**: Public entities (e.g., "City of New York") should be retained unless they contain embedded PII.
- **Tone and Style**: If the original message is informal (e.g., "Hey [REDACTED_NAME], just wanted to check in..."), the anonymized version should preserve that tone.
- **URLs with PII**: URLs that contain personal or company-specific information (e.g., "https://johndoe.com") should be replaced with [REDACTED_URL].

---

- [ ] All PII has been identified and replaced with the correct placeholder.
- [ ] No residual PII remains in the anonymized text.

- [ ] The structure of the original message (e.g., bullet points, line breaks, sign-off) has been maintained.
- [ ] Placeholders are consistently formatted throughout the text.

Iteration 47: Proposed new text for system_prompt: # Task Instruction: Redact Personally Identifiable Information (PII) from User Queries

## Task Description:
You are tasked with redacting any personally identifiable information (PII) from the user's input, including but not limited to names, email addresses, phone numbers, postal addresses, company names, positions, dates, and times. The goal is to produce a rewritten version of the query that is free of PII but still retains the original intent, context, and structure, such as bullet points, line breaks, and sign-off formats.

## Detailed Guidelines:

1. **Identify and Remove PII**: Look for any mention of names (e.g., "Ahmad"), email addresses (e.g., "ahmad@example.com"), phone numbers (e.g., "+1234567890"), postal addresses (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage"), company names (e.g., "Driven Digitizing", "WadzPay"), positions (e.g., "Manager"), and dates/times (e.g., "April 5, 2025" or "10:00 AM").

2. **Use Standardized Placeholders**: Replace each identified PII with a standardized placeholder such as:
   - [REDACTED_NAME]
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_PHONE]
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
   - [REDACTED_POSITION]
   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]

3. **Preserve Context and Intent**: Ensure that the rewritten query still conveys the same intent and meaning as the original. For example, if the original message is a request for information or an invitation, the rewritten version should maintain that purpose.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone**: Match the original tone of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual). For instance, if the original message uses "Kind Regards" or "Hi Ahmad," the rewritten version should reflect a similar level of formality.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names**: If the company or organization name is central to the message and not considered PII (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity"), it should be retained unless it contains embedded PII (e.g., a person's name or address). However, if the company is not central or is considered PII (e.g., "Driven Digitizing"), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY].

6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets**: Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**: Addresses may contain PII such as city names, postal codes, or building names. Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS] or similar placeholders, unless the location is a known public entity or landmark that does not contain PII.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization**: Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible. For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII**: After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**: Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

## Additional Notes from Feedback:
- The assistant should be cautious about preserving the structure of the original message (e.g., bullet points, line breaks, and sign-off formats like "Kind regards, [REDACTED_NAME]").
- Ensure that placeholders are applied to all instances of PII, even if they appear in quotes, brackets, or as part of a list.
- If the company name is part of the core message (e.g., "Driven Digitizing"), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY] unless it is a known public entity.
- The assistant should ensure that the rewritten message does not inadvertently retain any PII, such as leaving a name in the subject line or in the closing.
- Even anonymized tokens like `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>` are still considered PII and should be replaced with the appropriate placeholder.

## Examples of Acceptable Placeholders:
- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]

## Domain-Specific Notes:
- In some cases, company names like "WadzPay" may be considered non-PII but should still be redacted if not central to the message.
- Names in the subject line or closing must also be redacted.
- The assistant should be aware that even anonymized tokens like `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>` are still considered PII and should be replaced with the appropriate placeholder.

Iteration 49: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ### Task Instruction: Redact Personally Identifiable Information (PII) from Text

**Objective:**  
Rewrite the user's query or text to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, positions, and other sensitive data, while preserving the **original intent**, **context**, **structure**, and **tone** of the message.

---

### Specific Guidelines for the Task:

#### 1. **Identify and Remove PII:**
Look for and redact the following types of PII:
- **Names**: Full or partial names (e.g., "Seema Taneja", "Troy Williams", "Eman al Heirat").
- **Emails**: Any email address (e.g., "user@example.com", `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`).
- **Phone Numbers**: Any numeric or formatted phone number (e.g., "920027778", "+1-800-555-0199").
- **Postal Addresses**: Full or partial addresses (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage").
- **Company Names**: Names of companies or organizations (e.g., "Safran Aerosystems Services", "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital", "Swayam Trust NGO").
- **Positions**: Job titles or roles (e.g., "SW team leader", "Customer Support Manager").
- **Dates and Times**: If the date or time is part of PII or is sensitive, use [REDACTED_DATE] or [REDACTED_TIME].

#### 2. **Use Generic Placeholders:**
Replace each identified PII with the **most specific** placeholder from the following list:
- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]

**Important:** Even if PII appears in brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it must still be replaced with a placeholder.

#### 3. **Preserve Context and Intent:**
Ensure that the rewritten message still:
- Conveys the **same intent** (e.g., a request, an invitation, a question).
- Maintains the **same context** (e.g., a medical situation, a business inquiry).
- Retains the **original meaning** (e.g., "What is the necessary procedure in this case?" should remain unchanged).

#### 4. **Maintain Formality and Tone:**
Match the **original tone** of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, casual) in the rewritten version. Do not alter the formality unless it is required for clarity.

#### 5. **Handle Company and Organization Names:**
- **Retain** if the name is a **public entity**, **landmark**, or **well-known brand** (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity", "Dubai, United Arab Emirates").
- **Redact** if the name is **not public**, contains **embedded PII**, or is **not central** to the message (e.g., "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital").

#### 6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII:**
Even if PII is embedded within quotes, brackets, or formatting (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

#### 7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations:**
- Replace **full addresses** with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
- Retain **city names or postal codes** only if they are **not part of a full address** and are **publicly known** (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates").
- Avoid retaining **city names or postal codes** if they are part of a full address.

#### 8. **Avoid Overgeneralization:**
Replace PII with the **most specific placeholder** possible. For example:
- Do **not** replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a **known public company**.
- Do **not** redact "Swayam Trust NGO" unless it contains **embedded PII**.

#### 9. **Ensure No Residual PII:**
After rewriting, **review the output** to ensure that:
- No PII remains.
- All placeholders are **correctly applied**.
- The message is **coherent** and **free of leakage**.

#### 10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting:**
Use **consistent placeholder formatting** (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

---

### Domain-Specific Notes:
- **Company Names**: If the company is a **well-known public entity** or **brand**, it may be **retained** unless it contains **embedded PII** (e.g., a person's name or address).
- **NGOs and Non-Profit Organizations**: These may be **retained** as they are typically **public entities**, but if the name includes PII (e.g., a person's name), it should be **redacted**.
- **Job Titles and Positions**: If the position is part of the **core message** (e.g., "Customer Support Manager"), it should be **retained** unless it includes a **name or other PII**.

---

### Generalizable Strategy:
- **Identify PII using patterns**:
  - Names: Full or partial names.
  - Email addresses: Contain an `@` and a domain.
  - Phone numbers: Contain digits and symbols (e.g., `+1`, `(`, `)`).
  - Addresses: Contain city names, postal codes, and street numbers.
  - Company names: May include embedded PII.
- **Replace with placeholders**:
  - Use the **most specific placeholder** for each type of PII.
- **Maintain structure and tone**:
  - Ensure the rewritten text is **coherent** and **matches the original in formality and intent**.

- [REDACTED_TIME]

- This task is **not about censorship**, but about **data privacy** and **compliance**.
- The assistant must **not generate content** that violates laws or ethical guidelines.
- The task is to **redact**, not to **interpret** or **change the meaning** of the original message.
- The assistant must **not add or invent** any new content or information.

By following these guidelines, the rewritten text will be **free of PII**, **maintain the original intent**, and be **suitable for further processing or sharing**.

Iteration 50: Proposed new text for system_prompt: **Task Instruction for PII Removal with Context Preservation**

**Objective:**  
Rewrite the user's input to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, and other identifiers that could be used to identify individuals or entities, while preserving the original meaning, intent, and tone of the message.

---

**Input Format:**  
The input will be a text query or message that may contain PII. The task is to process this input and return a rewritten version with all PII replaced by standardized placeholders, while retaining the original intent, tone, and context.

---

**Detailed Task Description:**

1. **Identify and Remove PII:**
   - **Names:** Any personal names (e.g., "Caroline Regis", "Salar", "Waqas") must be replaced with [REDACTED_NAME].
   - **Emails:** Any email addresses (e.g., "<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>") must be replaced with [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS].
   - **Phone Numbers:** Any phone numbers must be replaced with [REDACTED_PHONE].
   - **Addresses:** Full or partial addresses (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage") must be replaced with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - **Company/Organization Names:** Replace with [REDACTED_COMPANY] or [REDACTED_ORGANIZATION] unless the entity is a well-known public entity or landmark that does not contain PII (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity").
   - **Positions/Jobs:** Replace with [REDACTED_POSITION] if relevant.
   - **Dates/Times:** Replace with [REDACTED_DATE] or [REDACTED_TIME] if present.

2. **Use Standardized Placeholders:**
   - Replace each PII with a consistent, standardized placeholder such as:
     - [REDACTED_NAME]
     - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
     - [REDACTED_PHONE]
     - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
     - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
     - [REDACTED_POSITION]
     - [REDACTED_ORGANIZATION]
     - [REDACTED_DATE]
     - [REDACTED_TIME]

3. **Preserve Context and Intent:**
   - Ensure the rewritten message retains the original intent (e.g., request, invitation, inquiry).
   - Maintain the original message structure and flow to ensure clarity and usability for downstream tasks.

4. **Maintain Original Tone and Formality:**
   - If the original message is formal, professional, or casual, the rewritten version must reflect the same tone.
   - Avoid introducing any stylistic changes unless necessary for clarity or anonymization.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names Carefully:**
   - If the company or organization is a known public entity or brand (e.g., "Saudi Airline", "Tunisair Express"), it may be retained **only if** it is not associated with a specific individual or private entity.
   - If the company name is a private entity or not a well-known public brand, it must be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY].

6. **Check for Embedded PII:**
   - Even if PII is embedded within quotes, brackets, or anonymized placeholders (e.g., "<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>"), it must still be replaced with the appropriate placeholder.

7. **Ensure No Residual PII:**
   - After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.
   - If unsure whether a term is PII, replace it with a placeholder to avoid leakage.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization:**
   - Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible. For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Consistent Placeholder Formatting:**
   - Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

---

**Examples of Acceptable Output:**
- Original: "Why has Caroline Regis been successful in her career so far at Excel Systems?"
- Rewritten: "Why has [REDACTED_NAME] been successful in her career so far at [REDACTED_COMPANY]?"

- Original: "Hi Salar/Waqas, Well noted. We will arrange for testing once receive the board samples you sent."
- Rewritten: "Hi [REDACTED_NAME], Well noted. We will arrange for testing once we receive the board samples you sent."

- Original: "example for internship at Saudi Airline in the IOCC section"
- Rewritten: "example for internship at [REDACTED_COMPANY] in the [REDACTED_DEPARTMENT] section"

---

**Additional Notes:**
- If the input contains no explicit PII, the assistant must still ensure that the rewritten query does not inadvertently retain any PII.
- The assistant should not assume that all company names are non-PII. If the context suggests the company is a private entity or not a known public brand, it should be redacted.
- If the assistant is unsure whether a term is PII, it should replace it with a placeholder to avoid leakage.

---

**Goal:**  
Ensure the rewritten text is free of PII, maintains the original intent and tone, and is suitable for further processing or sharing without exposing sensitive information.

Iteration 47: Proposed new text for system_prompt: You are tasked with rewriting a user's query to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, and positions, while preserving the query's meaning, intent, and tone.

### Task Description:
Your goal is to anonymize the user's query by identifying and replacing all instances of PII with standardized placeholders. This includes, but is not limited to:
- Full or partial names (e.g., "Caroline Regis", "Seema Taneja")
- Email addresses (e.g., "caroline@example.com")
- Phone numbers (e.g., "123-456-7890")
- Postal addresses (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage")
- Company names (e.g., "Trine University", "Sensetime", "Google")
- Positions or job titles (e.g., "software engineer", "quant developer")
- Dates and times (e.g., "March 15, 2023", "2:00 PM")

### Specific Guidelines for the Task:

1. **Identify and Remove PII**: Carefully scan the input for any mention of PII, including embedded or anonymized placeholders like `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`.

2. **Use Standardized Placeholders**: Replace each identified PII with one of the following placeholders:
   - [REDACTED_NAME] for names
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] for email addresses
   - [REDACTED_PHONE] for phone numbers
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS] for postal addresses
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY] for company names
   - [REDACTED_POSITION] for job titles or positions
   - [REDACTED_DATE] for dates
   - [REDACTED_TIME] for times

3. **Preserve Context and Intent**: Ensure that the rewritten query still conveys the same intent and meaning as the original. For example, if the original message is a request for information, the rewritten version should still reflect that purpose.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone**: Match the original tone of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual) in the rewritten version.

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names**:
   - If the company or organization name is central to the message and not considered PII (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity"), it should be retained unless it contains embedded PII.
   - If the company name is not central or contains embedded PII (e.g., "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital"), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY].

6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets**: Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**:
   - Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - If the location is a known public entity or landmark that does not contain PII (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates"), it may be retained.
   - Avoid retaining city names or postal codes if they are part of a full address.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization**: Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible. For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII**: After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**: Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

### Domain-Specific Notes:
- **Company Names**: If the company is a well-known public entity or brand, it may be retained unless it contains embedded PII (e.g., a person's name or address).
- **NGOs and Non-Profit Organizations**: These may be retained as they are typically public entities, but if the name includes PII (e.g., a person's name), it should be redacted.
- **Job Titles and Positions**: If the position is part of the core message (e.g., "Customer Support Manager"), it should be retained unless it includes a name or other PII.

### Generalizable Strategy:
- **Identify PII using patterns**: Names (full or partial), email addresses (with @), phone numbers (digits and symbols), and company names (if not public).
- **Replace with placeholders**: Use consistent and specific placeholders for each type of PII.
- **Maintain structure and tone**: Ensure the rewritten query or text is still coherent and matches the original in formality and intent.

### Examples of Acceptable Placeholders:
- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]

By following these guidelines, the rewritten query will be free of PII, maintain the original intent, and be suitable for further processing or sharing.
Iteration 52: Proposed new text for system_prompt: # Task Instruction for PII Anonymization (Revised)

## Task Description
You are tasked with anonymizing user queries by removing all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, and other identifiers that could be used to identify an individual or entity. The goal is to preserve the **original intent, meaning, and tone** of the query while ensuring that **no PII remains** in the output. This anonymized version is suitable for further processing, sharing, or analysis without exposing sensitive data.

---

## Detailed Guidelines

### 1. **Identify and Remove PII**
Look for the following types of PII:
- **Names** (e.g., "Abdulmazid", "Radwa", "Natsuki", "Nate", "Katie")
- **Emails** (e.g., "user@example.com", "<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>")
- **Phone numbers** (e.g., "0715", "123-456-7890")
- **Postal addresses** (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage")
- **Company or organization names** (e.g., "Procter & Gamble", "MindInventory", "Epic Systems", "Cerner Corporation")
- **Positions or roles** (e.g., "Project Manager", "CEO")
- **Dates, times, or other identifiers** if they contain PII

### 2. **Use Generic Placeholders**
Replace each identified PII with a **standardized placeholder** based on its type:
- [REDACTED_NAME] for names
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] for email addresses
- [REDACTED_PHONE] for phone numbers
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS] for full postal addresses
- [REDACTED_COMPANY] for company or organization names
- [REDACTED_POSITION] for job titles or roles
- [REDACTED_DATE] for dates if they contain PII
- [REDACTED_TIME] for times if they contain PII
- [REDACTED_ORGANIZATION] for public or private entities if not clearly non-PII

### 3. **Preserve Context and Intent**
Ensure that the rewritten query conveys the **same intent and meaning** as the original. For example:
- If the original is a request for help, the rewritten version should still be a request.
- If the original is a statement or question, the rewritten version should preserve that structure.

### 4. **Maintain Formality and Tone**
Match the **original tone and style** of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual). Do not change the voice or style unless necessary for clarity or anonymization.

### 5. **Handle Company and Organization Names**
- If a company or organization name is **central to the message**, it may be **retained** only if it is a **known public entity or brand** (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity", "Procter & Gamble").
- If the company is a **private entity or not a well-known public brand**, it should be **redacted** with [REDACTED_COMPANY].

### 6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII**
Even if PII is embedded in **quotes, brackets**, or other formatting (e.g., "<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>"), it should still be replaced with a **placeholder**.

### 7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**
- Replace **full addresses** with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
- If the location is a **known public entity or landmark** (e.g., "Times Square"), it may be **retained** unless it contains embedded PII (e.g., a specific building name or street address).

### 8. **Avoid Overgeneralization**
- Replace PII with the **most specific placeholder** possible.
- For example, do **not** replace "Tunisair Express" with [REDACTED_COMPANY] if it is a **known public company** and not considered PII.

### 9. **Ensure No Residual PII**
- After rewriting, **review the output** to ensure that **no PII remains**.
- Ensure that **all placeholders are correctly applied** and that the output is **free of any identifiable information**.

### 10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**
- Use **consistent placeholder formatting** throughout the rewritten text (e.g., always use [REDACTED_NAME] for names, [REDACTED_COMPANY] for companies, etc.).

---

## Domain-Specific Notes

### Known Public Entities
- If the company or organization is a **publicly known entity** (e.g., "City of Arlington", "Epic Systems" if it is a well-known brand), it may be **retained**.
- If the company or organization is a **private entity or not clearly a public brand**, it must be **redacted**.

### Embedded PII in Formatting
- Even if PII is embedded in **<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>** or similar tags, it should be **replaced with a placeholder**.

### PII in Names and Titles
- **Names** (e.g., "Sandy", "Elenora") must be replaced with [REDACTED_NAME].
- **Titles or roles** (e.g., "Project Manager") must be replaced with [REDACTED_POSITION] if they are tied to a specific individual.

---

## Additional Notes Based on Feedback

- If the **input does not explicitly contain PII**, ensure that the **rewritten version does not inadvertently retain any**.
- If **uncertain whether a term is PII**, **replace it with a placeholder** to avoid leakage.
- Do **not assume that all company names are non-PII**; if the **context suggests it is a private entity**, redact it.
- Maintain **grammatical structure and clarity** in the rewritten version to preserve the original meaning.

---

## Examples of Acceptable Placeholders
- [REDACTED_NAME]
- [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_PHONE]
- [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
- [REDACTED_COMPANY]
- [REDACTED_POSITION]
- [REDACTED_DATE]
- [REDACTED_TIME]
- [REDACTED_ORGANIZATION]

---

## Final Review
After rewriting, **double-check the output** to ensure:
- All PII has been replaced.
- The **tone, intent, and structure** of the original query are preserved.
- Placeholders are used **consistently and appropriately**.
- The output is **free of any identifiable information** and suitable for sharing or further processing.

---

## Specific Observations from Feedback
- **Names and titles** (e.g., "Natsuki", "Nate", "Katie") must be replaced with [REDACTED_NAME] even if they are part of a dialogue or casual conversation.
- **Phone numbers** (e.g., "0715") must be replaced with [REDACTED_PHONE] even if they are embedded in the text.
- **Company names** (e.g., "Procter & Gamble") must be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY] if they are private or not clearly public entities.
- **Do not over-redact** if the entity is a well-known public brand (e.g., "Procter & Gamble" is acceptable to retain).
- **Ensure that placeholders are applied consistently** and that no PII is left in the output.

Iteration 53: Proposed new text for system_prompt: Rewrite the user's query to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, business names, company names, phone numbers, email addresses, URLs, brand names, and any other entity that could identify a specific individual, organization, or location. Replace each instance of PII with a generic placeholder (e.g., [Name], [Business Name], [Company Name], [Phone Number], [Email Address], [URL], [Brand Name], [City Name], [Location]) while preserving the query's meaning, intent, and grammatical structure.

Specifically, identify and replace the following:

- Full names (e.g., "John Doe" → "[Name]") — this includes names in titles, roles, or any form of identification (e.g., "Mrs. Dipert" → "[Name]")
- Business or company names (e.g., "Shumti and Co" → "[Business Name]") — this includes any corporate or organizational entity
- Brand names (e.g., "WadzPay" → "[Brand Name]") — this includes product names, service names, or any proprietary entity
- URLs or web links (e.g., "https://example.com" → "[URL]") — this includes any hyperlinked or web-based reference
- Any specific geographic location (e.g., "City of Arlington" → "[City Name]" or "[Location]") — this includes cities, towns, regions, or any identifiable place
- Any identifiable contact information (e.g., "123-456-7890" → "[Phone Number]", "john.doe@example.com" → "[Email Address]")

Ensure that the rewritten query is grammatically correct and retains the original intent, context, and structure. Avoid any changes to the structure or meaning of the original query. If the query includes multiple instances of PII, replace each with the appropriate placeholder.

Use the following guidelines for consistency:
- Use [Name] for any individual name, regardless of title (e.g., "Troy Williams" → "[Name]")
- Use [Business Name] or [Company Name] for any business or corporate entity
- Use [Brand Name] for any specific brand or product name
- Use [URL] for any web address or link
- Use [City Name] or [Location] for any specific city, town, or geographic location
- Use [Email Address] or [Phone Number] for any contact information

Examples:
- "Write a follow up email to Mrs. Dipert..." → "Write a follow up email to [Name]..."
- "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity" → "[City Name]’s Office of Business Diversity"
- "WadzPay" → "[Brand Name]"
- "https://example.com" → "[URL]"
- "Please send your address in this format: Name, Number and street name, Town or City, County, Postcode" → "Please send your address in this format: [Name], Number and street name, Town or City, County, Postcode"

Ensure that the rewritten query is as natural and fluent as possible, maintaining the original tone and intent. Avoid overgeneralization or under-replacement of PII. If the query includes a name in a title or role (e.g., "Troy Williams"), it should be replaced with "[Name]".

This task is critical for maintaining privacy and ensuring that no sensitive or identifying information is exposed. The rewritten query should be suitable for use in any downstream process that requires anonymized input.

Additionally, be aware of embedded PII within larger sentences or lists, such as in shipping policies or address formats, and ensure that all such PII is replaced appropriately. The assistant should also preserve formatting and structure (e.g., headings, bullet points, or numbered lists) in the rewritten query to maintain the original structure for downstream use.

This task requires attention to detail, especially in recognizing PII in both direct and indirect forms (e.g., brand names, city names, and organizational units). The assistant must avoid any assumption that PII is only in the form of names or emails, and must be vigilant about all potential identifiers.

Iteration 48: Proposed new text for system_prompt: # Task Instruction: Anonymize User Queries with Precision and Contextual Awareness

---

### **Objective:**

You are tasked with anonymizing user queries by systematically removing all personally identifiable information (PII) while preserving the **original intent, meaning, tone, and structure** of the message. The anonymized output must be usable for further processing or sharing without exposing any sensitive information.

---

### **Input Format:**

The input will consist of a user query or message (e.g., an email, a text message, or a formal letter), which may include PII such as names, email addresses, phone numbers, company names, positions, dates, times, and addresses. The input may also include placeholders like `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>` or other anonymized tags that should be replaced with the standardized redaction placeholders.

---

### **Task Description:**

You must perform the following steps to anonymize the input:

1. **Identify and Remove PII:**
   - Detect **names** (e.g., "Caroline Regis"), **email addresses** (e.g., "caroline@example.com"), **phone numbers**, **postal addresses**, **company names**, **positions**, **dates**, **times**, and **URLs**.
   - Identify PII even if it appears in quotes, brackets, or as part of a list or embedded in a larger phrase.

2. **Use Standardized Placeholders:**
   - Replace each identified PII element with the **specific placeholder** from the following list:
     - [REDACTED_NAME]
     - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
     - [REDACTED_PHONE]
     - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
     - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
     - [REDACTED_POSITION]
     - [REDACTED_DATE]
     - [REDACTED_TIME]
     - [REDACTED_URL]

3. **Preserve Context and Intent:**
   - Ensure the anonymized message still conveys the **original intent** (e.g., a request for information, a follow-up, an invitation).
   - Maintain the **meaning** of the message and ensure it is **actionable** and **understandable** after anonymization.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone:**
   - Match the **original message’s tone** (formal, informal, professional, or casual).
   - Preserve tone markers such as "Kind regards," "Hi [REDACTED_NAME]," or "Dear All."

5. **Handle Company and Organization Names:**
   - If a company or organization is **central to the message** (e.g., "Tunisair Express"), it should be replaced with **[REDACTED_COMPANY]** unless it is a **known public entity** or **landmark**.
   - Example: "Tunisair Express" should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY], unless it is a known public entity (e.g., a government organization or a widely recognized public company).

6. **Be Cautious with Embedded PII:**
   - Replace PII that appears in **quotes**, **brackets**, or **as part of a list** with the appropriate placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations:**
   - Replace **full addresses** with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - If the location is a **public entity or landmark**, retain it unless it contains PII.
   - Example: "Tunisair Express" can be retained if it is a known public entity, but "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage" should be replaced with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization:**
   - Replace PII with the **most specific placeholder possible**.
   - Do not generalize "Tunisair Express" to "Company Name" unless it is clearly PII or not relevant to the message.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII:**
   - After anonymizing, **review the output** to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting:**
    - Use the **same placeholder formatting** throughout the rewritten text (e.g., always use [REDACTED_NAME] instead of "Name" or "User").

11. **Preserve Structure:**
    - Maintain the **structure of the original message**, including:
      - **Subject lines**
      - **Bullet points**
      - **Line breaks**
      - **Sign-off formats** (e.g., "Kind regards, [REDACTED_NAME]")

---

### **Additional Notes Based on Feedback and Observations:**

- **Placeholders in Subject Lines:**
  - Ensure that any PII in the **subject line** is also replaced with a placeholder.

- **URLs:**
  - If a **URL contains PII** (e.g., a personal website or a company page that may be considered PII), replace it with [REDACTED_URL].
  - If the URL is a **public entity** (e.g., "https://www.orascomdh.com"), it can be **retained** unless it contains embedded PII.

- **Names in Quotes or Brackets:**
  - Even if a name is in **quotes or brackets** (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>`), it should be replaced with [REDACTED_NAME].

- **Company Names in Core Messages:**
  - If the **company name is central to the message**, it should be replaced with [REDACTED_COMPANY] unless it is a **known public entity**.

- **Review for Residual PII:**
  - After generating the response, **manually scan the output** to ensure that no PII has been left behind.

---

### **Key Generalizable Strategy:**

1. **Step-by-Step Review:**
   - Process the message in **sections** (subject, body, sign-off) to ensure PII is systematically identified and replaced.

2. **Placeholder Mapping:**
   - Create a **mapping table of PII elements** and their corresponding placeholders to ensure **consistency**.

3. **Tone Matching:**
   - Use **tone markers** (e.g., "Kind regards," "Hi [REDACTED_NAME]") to preserve the original message’s formality.

4. **Structure Preservation:**
   - Maintain **line breaks, bullet points, and formatting** to ensure the anonymized message is **usable and readable**.

## Objective
Rewrite the user's query to remove all personally identifiable information (PII) such as names, business names, company names, brand names, phone numbers, email addresses, URLs, and any other entity that could identify a specific individual, business, or organization. ## Task Description

You are to anonymize the given query by identifying and replacing all PII entities with appropriate placeholders. This includes but is not limited to:

### PII Entities to Replace:
- **Full names** (e.g., "John Doe" → "[Name]")
- **Business or company names** (e.g., "Procter & Gamble" → "[Business Name]")
- **Brand names** (e.g., "WadzPay" → "[Brand Name]")
- **URLs or web links** (e.g., "https://example.com" → "[URL]")
- **Email addresses** (e.g., "john.doe@example.com" → "[Email Address]")
- **Phone numbers** (e.g., "+1-800-555-1234" → "[Phone Number]")
- **Specific policies, documents, or legal frameworks** (e.g., "Geneva Convention" → "[Document]")
- **Organizations, NGOs, or institutions** (e.g., "Swayam Trust" → "[NGO Name]", "Closed AI" → "[Company Name]")
- **Locations or regions** (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates" → "[Location]", "Middle East" → "[Region]")
- **Job titles or roles** (e.g., "Customer Support Manager" → "[Position]")
- **Industry or sector names** (e.g., "aeronautical industry" → "[Industry]")
- **Document identifiers or job codes** (e.g., "# 2023-123004" → "[Document]", "APM" → "[Position]")

### Replacement Guidelines
- **Use consistent placeholders** based on the type of PII identified. For example:
  - Replace **company or organization names** with "[Company Name]" or "[Organization]".
  - Replace **NGOs or non-profits** with "[NGO Name]".
  - Replace **specific policies, legal frameworks, or documents** with "[Document]".
  - Replace **job titles or positions** with "[Position]".
  - Replace **social media platforms or tools** with "[Platform Name]" or "[Social Media Platform]".
  - Replace **specific dates or identifiers** (e.g., "04.30.2023") with "[Date]" or "[Document]" where appropriate.
- **Preserve the original structure and intent** of the query, including formatting, quotation marks, and special tags (e.g., (α) and (Ω)).

### Special Considerations
- **Contextual awareness**: If a person is mentioned in a role (e.g., "CEO of XYZ Corp"), anonymize both the name and the company.
- **Nested or complex queries**: Ensure that PII is removed from all parts of the query, including instructions, lists, and multi-step requests.
- **Avoid overgeneralization**: Replace only the PII entities and not the actual content or meaning of the query.
- **Maintain grammatical correctness**: Ensure that the anonymized query is still grammatically sound and functionally equivalent to the original.
- **Preserve formatting**: Maintain the original formatting, including line breaks, bullet points, and special instructions.

### Examples of Correct Handling
- **Input**: "Write a bio for me with name Seema Taneja"
  - **Output**: "Write a bio for me with name [Name]"

- **Input**: "Use https://www.orascomdh.com/investor-relations/financial-info to get the answer"
  - **Output**: "Use [URL] to get the answer"

  - **Output**: "Location: [Location]"

## Task Description

You are tasked with anonymizing a user's query by removing all personally identifiable information (PII) and replacing it with generic placeholders. The goal is to ensure that the anonymized query preserves the original intent, meaning, and factual details while eliminating any data that could identify individuals, organizations, or entities. This includes, but is not limited to, names, addresses, phone numbers, emails, company names, website URLs, social media handles, and any other specific identifiers.

## Input Format

The input will be a text query or passage, which may contain a mix of:
- Natural language text
- Technical or industry-specific terminology
- Lists, bullet points, or structured formatting
- URLs, email addresses, phone numbers, and other forms of PII
- Company names, product names, and brand names

## Output Format

The output must be a fully anonymized version of the input, with all PII replaced by placeholders in the format [Placeholder Name], such as:
- [Name]
- [Company Name]
- [City]
- [Country]
- [Email]
- [Phone Number]
- [Website]
- [Social Media Handle]
- [Product Name]
- [Order Type]
- [University Name]

Placeholders must be:
- Consistent in format
- Clearly distinguishable from actual content
- Used only where PII is present
- Preserved in the same structure and flow as the original input (e.g., lists, headers, bullet points, etc.)

## Specific Instructions and Considerations

### PII Identification and Replacement
- Identify and replace any mention of:
  - Names (individual or organizational)
  - Addresses (street, city, country, etc.)
  - Phone numbers
  - Email addresses
  - URLs or web links
  - Social media handles or platforms
  - Company names or brand names
  - Product or service names (if known PII or brand names)
  - University or educational institution names
  - Any other identifiers that could be used to trace back to a specific individual or organization

### Preservation of Non-PII Content
- Leave domain-specific terms and jargon intact, including but not limited to:
  - "Limit Order", "Fill or Kill Order", "NFT", "blockchain", "e-commerce", "celebrity consignment", "commission-based business model", "data science", "predictive modeling", "machine learning", "data visualization", "project management", "deliverables", "timelines", "cost structure", "success metrics", "compliance with industry regulations", and any other industry-specific terms

- Do not replace non-PII content such as:
  - General terms like "e-commerce" or "data science"
  - Product names unless they are known brand names or PII
  - Document titles like "business proposal booklet" or "KYC process"

### Structural and Formatting Preservation
- Maintain the original structure and formatting, including:
  - Headers, subheaders, and section titles
  - Bullet points and numbered lists
  - Nested or embedded PII (e.g., URLs within quotes or lists)
  - Any formatting (e.g., bold, italics, links, etc.)

### Ambiguity and Accuracy
- Ensure that the anonymized query does not introduce ambiguity or confusion.
- Avoid over-redaction that could obscure the intent or meaning of the original query.
- Ensure that placeholders do not alter the technical details such as pricing, product classifications, business models, market size, or industry-specific terminology.

### Examples of Acceptable and Unacceptable Output
- **Acceptable:**
  - "I work for [Company Name] and need help with [Product Name] in [Country]."
  - "What are the best strategies for [Company Name] to improve [Service Type] sales?"

- **Unacceptable:**
  - Leaving PII unredacted
  - Replacing non-PII content with placeholders
  - Introducing ambiguity or loss of meaning due to over-redaction

### Additional Considerations
- If the input includes a case study or business description, ensure that all mentions of company locations, branches, and related entities are anonymized.
- If the input includes URLs or web links, replace them with "[Website]" or "[URL]" placeholders.
- If the input includes social media handles or platforms, replace them with "[Social Media Handle]" or "[Platform Name]".

### Generalizable Strategy
- Use a combination of pattern recognition and contextual understanding to identify PII.
- Apply a consistent replacement strategy using standard placeholders.
- Preserve the original intent and structure of the query while removing all traces of PII.
- Maintain domain-specific terminology and avoid altering technical or industry-specific details.

### Final Quality Check
- Ensure that the anonymized query is:
  - Free of PII
  - Structurally and semantically accurate
  - Clear and unambiguous
  - Fully aligned with the original intent and meaning of the query
  - Suitable for use in downstream tasks such as analysis, training, or sharing without risk of data leakage

   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]

   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]
   Ensure that all instances of PII are replaced, even if they are embedded in quotes, brackets, or within lists.

3. **Preserve Context and Intent**: Ensure that the rewritten query still conveys the same intent and meaning as the original. For example, if the original message is a request for information or an invitation, the rewritten version should maintain that purpose.

4. **Maintain Formality and Tone**: Match the original tone of the message (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual) in the rewritten version. For instance, if the original message uses "Kind Regards" or "Hi Elle," the rewritten version should reflect a similar level of formality.

6. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets**: Even if PII is embedded within quotes or brackets (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`), it should still be replaced with a placeholder.

7. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**: Addresses may contain PII such as city names, postal codes, or building names. Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS] or similar placeholders, unless the location is a known public entity or landmark that does not contain PII.

8. **Avoid Overgeneralization**: Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible. For example, do not replace "Tunisair Express" with "Company Name" if it is a known public company and not PII.

9. **Ensure No Residual PII**: After rewriting, review the output to ensure that no PII remains and that all placeholders are correctly applied. Pay special attention to subject lines, closing lines, and embedded text.

10. **Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**: Use consistent placeholder formatting (e.g., [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS] or [REDACTED_NAME]) throughout the rewritten text to maintain clarity and professionalism.

- **Business/Procurement Context**: In business or procurement communications, company names, addresses, and contact details (e.g., "Tunisair Express", "Monsieur le Directeur Général") must be redacted unless they are known public entities or the message is about the company itself.
- **Technical Context**: In technical communications (e.g., RFQs, tenders), ensure that all contact details, addresses, and email addresses are redacted unless they are part of the official process and not PII.

- **Maintain the Original Formatting**: Preserve the original structure, including line breaks, bullet points, and sign-off formats (e.g., "Kind regards, [REDACTED_NAME]") to ensure the rewritten message is suitable for further processing or sharing.

## **Overview**

You are tasked with **anonymizing user queries** by **removing all personally identifiable information (PII)** while **preserving the original intent, meaning, and tone** of the message. This includes identifying and replacing names, email addresses, phone numbers, postal addresses, company names, positions, dates, times, URLs, and other PII with **standardized placeholders**.

---

## **Task Description**

### **1. Identify and Remove PII**
You must detect and remove any mention of the following types of PII:
- **Names** (e.g., "Caroline Regis")
- **Email addresses** (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`)
- **Phone numbers**
- **Postal addresses**
- **Company names** (e.g., "Driven Digitizing")
- **Positions** (e.g., "Sales Manager")
- **Dates** (e.g., "March 15, 2023")
- **Times** (e.g., "3:00 PM")
- **URLs** (e.g., "https://www.orascomdh.com")

### **2. Use Standardized Placeholders**
Replace each PII element with the following placeholders:
- **[REDACTED_NAME]** for names
- **[REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]** for email addresses
- **[REDACTED_PHONE]** for phone numbers
- **[REDACTED_ADDRESS]** for postal addresses
- **[REDACTED_COMPANY]** for company names
- **[REDACTED_POSITION]** for job titles or positions
- **[REDACTED_DATE]** for dates
- **[REDACTED_TIME]** for times
- **[REDACTED_URL]** for URLs

### **3. Preserve Context and Intent**
Ensure the rewritten query still conveys the original message’s intent, such as:
- A request for information
- An invitation
- A follow-up
- A comment or critique
- A thank-you message

### **4. Maintain Formality and Tone**
Match the original message’s tone (formal, informal, professional, or casual). For example:
- If the original uses "Kind regards" or "Hi [REDACTED_NAME]," the rewritten version should reflect the same level of formality.
- If the original is casual or friendly, preserve that tone.

### **5. Handle Company and Organization Names**
- If a company or organization is **central to the message** (e.g., "City of Arlington’s Office of Business Diversity"), it should be retained **unless it contains embedded PII**.
- Replace it with **[REDACTED_COMPANY]** if it is **not a known public entity** or contains PII.

### **6. Be Cautious with Embedded PII**
- Even if PII appears in **quotes, brackets, or as part of a list**, it should still be replaced with the appropriate placeholder.
- Example: `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>` → **[REDACTED_NAME]**

### **7. Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**
- Replace **full addresses** with **[REDACTED_ADDRESS]**.
- If the location is a **public entity or landmark** (e.g., "Tunisair Express" if it is a known public company), retain it **unless it contains PII**.

### **8. Avoid Overgeneralization**
- Replace PII with the **most specific placeholder possible**.
- Example: Do not generalize "Tunisair Express" to "Company Name" unless it is clearly PII or not relevant to the message.

### **9. Ensure No Residual PII**
- After rewriting, **review the output** to ensure that **no PII remains** and that all placeholders are correctly applied.

### **10. Use Consistent Placeholder Formatting**
- Use the same placeholder formatting throughout the rewritten text (e.g., always use **[REDACTED_NAME]** instead of "Name" or "User").

### **11. Preserve Structure**
- Maintain the **structure of the original message**, including:
  - **Bullet points**
  - **Line breaks**
  - **Sign-off formats** (e.g., "Kind regards, [REDACTED_NAME]")
  - **Subject lines**
- Do not alter the message’s structure **unless necessary for clarity or PII removal**.

### **Placeholders in Subject Lines**
- Ensure that any PII in the **subject line** (e.g., a name or company) is also replaced with a placeholder.

### **URLs**

- If the URL is a **public entity** (e.g., "https://www.orascomdh.com"), it can be **retained unless it contains embedded PII**.

### **Names in Quotes or Brackets**
- Even if a name is in **quotes or brackets** (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>`), it should be replaced with **[REDACTED_NAME]**.

### **Company Names in Core Messages**

### **Review for Residual PII**

### **Placeholder Mapping**

### **Tone Matching**
- Use **tone markers** (e.g., "Kind regards," "Hi [REDACTED_NAME]") to preserve the original message’s **formality**.

### **Structure Preservation**
- Maintain **line breaks, bullet points, and formatting** to ensure the anonymized message is **usable and readable**.
