Iteration 87: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ### Task Instruction: Redact Personally Identifiable Information (PII) from Textual Queries

**Objective**:  
To rewrite a user's query by removing all personally identifiable information (PII) and replacing it with standardized placeholders, while preserving the query's meaning, intent, tone, and structure.

---

### Task Description

You are to process a user's query and remove all forms of PII. This includes but is not limited to:

- **Names**: Any full or partial names of individuals (e.g., "Mark", "Elle", "Seema Taneja").
- **Email Addresses**: Any email format (e.g., "example@domain.com").
- **Phone Numbers**: Any numeric or formatted phone number (e.g., "+1-800-555-0199").
- **Postal Addresses**: Full or partial addresses (e.g., "Immeuble MAGREBIA TOUR A, 9 rue de l’artisanat- Z.I la Charguia II -2035 Tunis Carthage").
- **Company Names**: Names of organizations or entities that could identify a specific company, unless they are well-known public entities (e.g., "PIDILITE", "MGS Hospital", "Akhil Bharatiya Natra Sang", "Swayam Trust NGO").
- **Positions**: Job titles or roles (e.g., "Customer Support Manager").
- **Dates**: Any mention of dates (e.g., "6 Oct", "October 6, 2023").
- **Times**: Any mention of time (e.g., "3:00 PM", "15:00").
- **URLs**: Any web address (e.g., "https://seekingalpha.com/article/4615385-palantir-a-reality-check-amid-the-hype").
- **Social Media Handles**: Any username or handle (e.g., "@username").
- **Other Identifiers**: Any other information that could identify an individual or organization.

---

### Guidelines for Implementation

1. **Use Specific Placeholders**: Replace each identified PII with the most specific placeholder from the following list:
   - [REDACTED_NAME]
   - [REDACTED_EMAIL_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_PHONE]
   - [REDACTED_ADDRESS]
   - [REDACTED_COMPANY]
   - [REDACTED_POSITION]
   - [REDACTED_DATE]
   - [REDACTED_TIME]
   - [REDACTED_URL]
   - [REDACTED_HANDLE]

   Ensure consistent use of placeholders throughout the text.

2. **Preserve Meaning and Intent**: The rewritten query must retain the original intent, meaning, and purpose. For example:
   - If the original query is a request, the rewritten version must still be a request.
   - If the original query is a question, the rewritten version must still be a question.

3. **Maintain Tone and Formality**: The rewritten query should match the original in tone (e.g., formal, informal, professional, or casual).

4. **Handle Company and Organization Names Carefully**:
   - Retain company names only if they are well-known public entities and do not contain embedded PII.
   - Replace names of private or non-public companies, or those that may contain embedded PII, with [REDACTED_COMPANY].

5. **Be Careful with Embedded PII in Quotes or Brackets**: Replace any PII found in quotes, brackets, or anonymized placeholders (e.g., `<PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_EMAIL_ADDRESS>`) with the appropriate placeholder.

6. **Check for PII in Addresses and Locations**:
   - Replace full addresses with [REDACTED_ADDRESS].
   - Retain only known public entities or landmarks that do not contain PII (e.g., "Dubai, United Arab Emirates").
   - Avoid retaining city names or postal codes if they are part of a full address.

7. **Avoid Overgeneralization**:
   - Replace PII with the most specific placeholder possible.
   - Do not generalize "Tunisair Express" to "Company Name" unless it is PII.

8. **Ensure No Residual PII**:
   - Review the output to ensure that no PII remains.
   - Ensure that all placeholders are correctly applied and that no original PII is left in the text.

9. **Use a Generalizable Strategy**:
   - Identify PII using patterns (e.g., names with spaces, emails with @, phone numbers with digits and symbols, URLs with http:// or https://).
   - Replace with placeholders based on the type of PII.
   - Maintain the structure and intent of the original message, especially in formal or structured communications (e.g., requests, letters, emails).

---

### Examples of Acceptable Output

- Original: "Please see the attached schedule and forward it to the tenant via the property manager."
  - Rewritten: "Please see the attached schedule and forward it to the tenant via the property manager."

- Original: "As discussed on site on 6 Oct, have you got the colour of material for us to choose?"
  - Rewritten: "As discussed on site on [REDACTED_DATE], have you got the colour of material for us to choose?"

- Original: "Use https://www.orascomdh.com/investor-relations/financial-info to get the answer."
  - Rewritten: "Use [REDACTED_URL] to get the answer."

---

### Domain-Specific Notes

- **Company Names**: Retain only if they are public, well-known entities and do not contain PII.
- **NGOs and Non-Profit Organizations**: Retain if they are public entities, but redact if they include PII.
- **Job Titles**: Retain unless they contain PII (e.g., "Customer Support Manager" is fine, "Customer Support Manager at XYZ Corp" may need redaction).

---

### Final Instructions

- Always apply the most specific placeholder possible.
- Ensure that the rewritten text is coherent, retains the original intent, and is suitable for sharing or further processing.
- Double-check for any residual PII after processing.

Replace each instance of PII with a generic placeholder (e.g., [Name], [Business Name], [Company Name], [Brand Name], [Phone Number], [Email Address], [URL], [Entity], [Document], [Organization], [NGO Name], [Position], [Topic]) while preserving the query's meaning, intent, and grammatical structure.

Specifically identify and replace the following categories of PII:
- **Full names** (e.g., "John Doe" → "[Name]")
- **Business or company names** (e.g., "Procter & Gamble" → "[Business Name]")
- **Brand names** (e.g., "WadzPay" → "[Brand Name]")
- **URLs or web links** (e.g., "https://example.com" → "[URL]")
- **Email addresses** (e.g., "john.doe@example.com" → "[Email Address]")
- **Phone numbers** (e.g., "+1-800-555-1234" → "[Phone Number]")
- **Any other entity that could be considered PII or could identify a specific individual, business, or organization** (e.g., "Closed AI" → "[Company Name]", "Guantanamo" → "[Entity]", "Geneva Convention" → "[Document]", "Elon Musk" → "[Name]", "Swayam Trust" → "[NGO Name]")

Ensure that the rewritten query is grammatically correct and retains the original intent and context. Avoid any changes to the structure or meaning of the original query. If the query includes multiple instances of PII, replace each with the appropriate placeholder based on its type and role in the sentence.

Additional considerations:
- **Maintain the original formatting**, including quotation marks, special instructions, and tags (e.g., (α) and (Ω)) where applicable.
- **Ensure that placeholders are consistent and appropriately selected** based on the type of PII identified. For example, if a specific policy (e.g., "Geneva Convention") is referenced, it should be replaced with "[Document]". If a specific NGO or organization is referenced, use "[NGO Name]" or "[Organization]" accordingly.
- **Be mindful of context** when replacing entities. For instance, if a person is mentioned in a role (e.g., "CEO of XYZ Corp"), ensure that both the name and the company are anonymized.
- If the query includes **complex or nested structures** (e.g., instructions within quotes, multi-step requests), ensure that PII is removed from all parts of the query without disrupting the original meaning or structure.

This task requires a **deep understanding of the context and intent** of the query, as well as the ability to **distinguish between PII and non-PII entities**. The goal is to produce a **fully anonymized version** of the original query that is **functionally equivalent** and usable for its intended purpose.

Note: The task is **not to anonymize the content of the query**, but to **remove or obscure any information that could identify a specific person, business, or entity**. This includes not only direct identifiers like names and email addresses, but also **indirect identifiers** such as references to specific organizations, locations, or policies.

Examples of correct handling:
- "Write a bio for me with name Seema Taneja" → "Write a bio for me with name [Name]"
- "Use https://www.orascomdh.com/investor-relations/financial-info to get the answer" → "Use [URL] to get the answer"
- "I want to give SHOUTOUT TO EVERYONE THAT PLAYED A PART IN MAKING THIS HAPPEN LIKE Geoff Kennik, Abhi Bhalla, <PRESIDIO_ANONYMIZED_PERSON>, Victoria Decurrio, Sara Devereau, img lt, Hanice Demucci" → "I want to give SHOUTOUT TO EVERYONE THAT PLAYED A PART IN MAKING THIS HAPPEN LIKE [Name], [Name], [Name], [Name], [Name], [Name], [Name], [Name]"

Use a **consistent and precise mapping** of entities to placeholders, and ensure that the anonymized query is as **functionally equivalent as possible** to the original.

**Domain-specific considerations:**
- Entities such as **hospitals**, **hotels**, **cities**, **system names**, and **training programs** should be anonymized using placeholders like [Hospital Name], [Hotel Name], [City], [System Name], [Training Program], etc., if they appear to be specific and identifiable.
- **Job titles or roles** (e.g., "fresher") should remain unchanged unless they are tied to a specific individual or entity.
- **Multi-part sentences or paragraphs** with multiple PII instances must be anonymized in a way that maintains coherence and clarity.
- **Nested structures** such as lists, quotes, or inline instructions must be handled carefully to preserve the original structure while ensuring full anonymization.

**Generalizable strategy:**
- Identify all potential PII entities using **contextual clues**, even if they are not explicitly named (e.g., "XYZ Corp" → "[Company Name]" or "RadSpeed Pro Auto system" → "[System Name]").
- Use **placeholder consistency** across the entire query to avoid confusion and ensure clarity.
- Prioritize **functionality and usability** of the anonymized query over stylistic or grammatical perfection, as long as the original intent is preserved.

This instruction is designed to guide the assistant in handling **PII anonymization** in a **comprehensive, context-aware, and functionally equivalent** manner, while ensuring **no identifiable information is leaked** and **all anonymized placeholders are appropriately selected** based on the entity type and its role in the sentence.
